878|let's break down the clue:

- "landlord in london, perhaps" suggests that we are looking for a word that means a landlord and is associated with london. it could be a specific type of landlord or a common term for landlords in general.

- "found after a full" suggests that we need to combine two words: one meaning "found" or "available" and another word meaning "full" or "complete". the word for "found" or "available" should come before the word for "full" or "complete".

putting it all together, the answer is:

inn-keeper (7,6)

1617|flying v - the answer is "flying v" (6,3)
explanation: 
- "monumental barrage" refers to a barrage or a bombardment of something. 
- "put up by" indicates a reversal, so "barrage" is reversed to "egarrab". 
- "mother" refers to the abbreviation of "ma". 
- "vacuum cleaner" refers to "mother with vacuum cleaner" which is "m". 
- "in front" suggests that "m" should come before "egarrab", giving "megarrab". 
- together, "megarrab" sounds like "megarob", and in the context of the clue, it is referencing a type of electric guitar called "flying v".|hoover dam

4957|the clue "residence contains old loo" is a cryptic clue that requires a bit of analysis to solve.

firstly, let's break down the clue. 
- "residence" indicates a word that means a place where someone lives.
- "contains" suggests that we need to insert something inside that word.
- "old" indicates that we need an abbreviation to represent an old word.
- "loo" is a slang term for a toilet.

putting it all together, we can deduce that we need to find a word for a residence that contains an abbreviation for an old word and the term for a toilet.

the answer to this clue is "loo" (a toilet) being inserted into the word "den" (a word for a residence) to form the word "lodden" which means "residence". the number of characters (3,4) matches the number of characters in the word "lodden", which is 7.|how come

6347|now and then fielder in square cowered

the key to this clue is the phrase "fielder in square." this indicates that we need to find a word for a fielder that can be found inside a word for "square."

the word that fits this clue is "coward," which means someone who lacks courage or is easily frightened. now we need to find a word for "fielder" that can be found inside "coward."

the word for "fielder" is "ward." so, if we insert "ward" into "coward," we get "cowered."

therefore, the answer is "cowered" (7 characters).|quailed

15111|outside on the windy side suggests that we need to take a word for "meal" (4 letters) and place it outside another word for "blundered" (3 letters). 

the word for "meal" that fits is "mess". and the word for "blundered" that fits is "err".

so the answer is "errmess" which has 7 characters.|fluffed

15305|icemaid

explanation:
- "proverbially cold thing" refers to icy
- "heartless" indicates removing the middle letter 'y'
- "doctor" is often abbreviated as dr
- "laing" indicates removing the letters la
- "cruelly rejected" means reversing the word
- "girl" is often referred to as maid

putting it all together, we get icemaid which has 8 characters.|doornail

15897|sin we perceived "sin" to be the answer for the clue "adjacent tendons' central parts (3,2)"  because the word "adjacent" implies that two separate words of length 3 and 2 are combined. the word "tendons" indicates that we should look for a synonym for that word, which can be "sinew." taking the central parts (middle letters) of "sinew" gives us "si" and "n." thus, the solution is "sin" which has 3 characters.|end on

18431|stethose

the answer is "stethose".
explanation:
"twist" indicates an anagram.
"fish" is an anagram indicator.
"beneath medical tubes" suggests that "fish" should be placed beneath "medical tubes".
so taking the letters of "fish" and placing them beneath "medical tubes" (which is an anagram of "stethose") gives us "stethose".|entangle

19218|fisherman's item reverting to a story about catch initially is just a feeler (8)
answer: angler's
explanation:
the clue indicates that we are looking for a 8-letter word.

"fisherman's item" refers to an angler's tool or equipment.

"reverting to a story" indicates that we need to reverse the word "reel" (another fishing item) to get "leer".

"about catch initially" means we need to take the first letter of the word "catch", which is "c".

"just a feeler" is the definition of the word "angler's", which is a feeler or lure used in fishing.

therefore, the answer is angler's.|tentacle

21001|let's break down the clue:

"trays entirely fed" suggests that we need to find a word for trays or containers that is followed by a word meaning "entirely" or "completely".

"to guinea pigs, perhaps" suggests that the answer could be a word for animals that guinea pigs belong to, or a word related to guinea pigs in some way.

putting it together, we are looking for a seven-letter word that means trays or containers and is followed by a word related to guinea pigs.

the answer is "feeders" (7), with "feed" meaning trays or containers, and "ers" referring to the animals that guinea pigs belong to, rodents.|pallets

24953|the answer is "theories" because:
- "speculative" is the definition of the word.
- "by half" indicates that we need to take half of the word.
- "deposited in account" refers to the letters "de" being placed inside the word "theories" (after taking half of it).
- "after account" suggests that the remaining letters of the word "theories" (after taking half of it) should come after the letters "de".
therefore, the answer is "theories" which has 8 characters.|academic

"catching plenty" suggests that we take the word "wave" (as in ocean waves) and add the word "air" (as in catching air). "evans ultimately conceded bye" indicates that we need to remove the last letter ("s") from "evans" and add the word "bye" (as in saying goodbye). combine "wave" and "air" after removing the last letter from "evans", and we get "wavier" which means conceding bye or giving up.|toodle oo
